85 const double kOscBipolarModRangeSemitones = 12.0; // --> unipolar, 100%
86 #define ARC4RANDOMMAX 4294967295 // (2^32 - 1)
87 #define EXTRACT_BITS(the_val, bits_start, bits_len) ((the_val >> (bits_start - 1)) & ((1 << bits_len) - 1))

107 /* mmaMIDItoAtten()
108 calculates the raw attenuation according to MMA DLS spec
109 midiValue = the MIDI (0 -> 127) value to convert
110 */
111 inline double mmaMIDItoAtten(unsigned int midiValue)
112 {
113  if (midiValue == 0)
114  return 0.0; // --- floor
115 
116  return ((double)midiValue*(double)midiValue) / (127.0*127.0);
117 }
118 
119 /* calculatePanValues()
120 calculates the left and right pan values
121 dPanMod = bipolar (-1 -> 1) pan modulation value
122 returns are via pass-by-reference mechanism
123 */
124 inline void calculatePanValues(double bipolarModulator, double& leftPanValue, double& rightPanValue)
125 {
126  leftPanValue = cos((kPi / 4.0)*(bipolarModulator + 1.0));
127  rightPanValue = sin((kPi / 4.0)*(bipolarModulator + 1.0));
128 
129  leftPanValue = fmax(leftPanValue, (double)0.0);
130  leftPanValue = fmin(leftPanValue, (double)1.0);
131  rightPanValue = fmax(rightPanValue, (double)0.0);
132  rightPanValue = fmin(rightPanValue, (double)1.0);
133 }
134 
135 // --- quasi-random noise gnerator
136 inline double doPNSequence(uint32_t& uPNRegister)
137 {
138  // --- get the bits
139  uint32_t b0 = EXTRACT_BITS(uPNRegister, 1, 1); // 1 = b0 is FIRST bit from right
140  uint32_t b1 = EXTRACT_BITS(uPNRegister, 2, 1); // 1 = b1 is SECOND bit from right
141  uint32_t b27 = EXTRACT_BITS(uPNRegister, 28, 1); // 28 = b27 is 28th bit from right
142  uint32_t b28 = EXTRACT_BITS(uPNRegister, 29, 1); // 29 = b28 is 29th bit from right
143 
144  // --- form the XOR
145  uint32_t b31 = b0^b1^b27^b28;
146 
147  // --- form the mask to OR with the register to load b31
148  if (b31 == 1)
149  b31 = 0x10000000;
150 
151  // --- shift one bit to right
152  uPNRegister >>= 1;
153 
154  // --- set the b31 bit
155  uPNRegister |= b31;
156 
157  // --- convert the output into a floating point number, scaled by experimentation
158  // --- to a range of o to +2.0
159  float fOut = (float)(uPNRegister) / ((pow((float)2.0, (float)32.0)) / 16.0);
160 
161  // --- shift down to form a result from -1.0 to +1.0
162  fOut -= 1.0;
163 
164  return fOut;
165 }

199 struct ModInputData
200 {
201  ModInputData() { init(); }
202  ModInputData& operator=(const ModInputData& modulators) // need this override for collections to work
203  {
204  if (this == &modulators)
205  return *this;
206 
207  // --- bulk memory block copy (fast)
208  memcpy(&modulationInputs[0], &modulators.modulationInputs[0], MAX_MODULATION_CHANNELS * sizeof(double));
209 
210  modInputCount = modulators.modInputCount;
211 
212  return *this;
213  }
214 
215  // --- fast clearing of array
216  void clear() {
217  memset(modulationInputs, 0, MAX_MODULATION_CHANNELS * sizeof(double));
218  }
219 
220  // --- set defaults to avoid accidental note-off state
221  void init() {
222  modulationInputs[kEGMod] = 1.0;
223  modulationInputs[kAmpMod] = 1.0;
224  modulationInputs[kMaxDownAmpMod] = 1.0;
225  }
226 
227  // --- for modulation matrix to have instant access to the input array
228  double* getModuationInputPtr(unsigned int index) {
229  if (index < MAX_MODULATION_CHANNELS)
230  return &modulationInputs[index];
231  return nullptr;
232  }
233 
234  // --- array of inputs; for stereo 0 = LEFT and 1 = RIGHT
235  double modulationInputs[MAX_MODULATION_CHANNELS] = { 0.0 };
236 
237  // --- count, set by the voice that renders to let the engine know how many outputs are real
238  unsigned int modInputCount = 0; // the active number of mod inputs starting with channel[0]
239 };

319 // --- Global MIDI Enum - these are indexes of slots in the global MIDI table
320 //
321 // --- These are designed to look and behave as MIDI data, so it will either be
322 // 7-bits 0 ->127
323 // or
324 // 14-bits LSB|MSB
325 // 00 00 --> 0 or -8192
326 // 00 40 --> midpoint
327 // 7F 7F --> 16383 or +8191
328 enum globalMIDI {
329  kCurrentMIDINoteNumber, /* 7 bits 0 ->127 */
330  kCurrentMIDINoteVelocity, /* 7 bits 0 ->127 */
331  kLastMIDINoteNumber, /* 7 bits 0 ->127 */
332  kLastMIDINoteVelocity, /* 7 bits 0 ->127 */
333  kMIDIPitchBendDataLSB, /* 14 bit LSB */
334  kMIDIPitchBendDataMSB, /* 14 bit MSB */
335  kMIDIMasterPBSensCoarse, /* MSB: 7 bits 0 ->127 Semitones */
336  kMIDIMasterPBSensFine, /* LSB: 7 bits 0 ->127 cents */
337  kMIDIMasterTuneCoarseLSB, /* 14 bit LSB */
338  kMIDIMasterTuneCoarseMSB, /* 14 bit MSB */
339  kMIDIMasterTuneFineLSB, /* 14 bit LSB */
340  kMIDIMasterTuneFineMSB, /* 14 bit MSB */
341  kMIDIMasterVolumeLSB, /* 14 bit LSB */
342  kMIDIMasterVolumeMSB, /* 14 bit MSB */
343  kNumMIDIGlobals
344 }; // --- for global MIDI table

404 inline void boundMIDIValueByte(unsigned int& value)
405 {
406  value = fmin(value, 127);
407  value = fmax(value, 0);
408 }

428 inline void boundIntValue(int& value, int min, int max)
429 {
430  value = fmin(value, max);
431  value = fmax(value, min);
432 }
433 
439 inline void mapDoubleValue(double& value, double min, double max, double minMap, double maxMap)
440 {
441  // --- bound to limits
442  value = fmin(value, max);
443  value = fmax(value, min);
444 
445  double mapped = ((value - min) / (max - min)) * (maxMap - minMap) + minMap;
446  value = mapped;
447 }
448 
449 
457 inline void mapIntValue(int& value, int min, int max, int minMap, int maxMap, bool roundValue = true)
458 {
459  // --- bound to limits
460  value = fmin(value, max);
461  value = fmax(value, min);
462 
463  double mapped = (double(value - min) / double(max - min)) * double(maxMap - minMap) + double(minMap);
464  if (roundValue)
465  value = (int)(round(mapped));
466  else
467  value = (int)mapped;
468 }
469 
477 inline void mapUintValue(unsigned int& value, unsigned int min, unsigned int max, unsigned int minMap, unsigned int maxMap, bool roundValue = true)
478 {
479  // --- bound to limits
480  value = fmin(value, max);
481  value = fmax(value, min);
482 
483  double mapped = (double(value - min) / double(max - min)) * double(maxMap - minMap) + double(minMap);
484  if (roundValue)
485  value = (unsigned int)(round(mapped));
486  else
487  value = (unsigned int)mapped;
488 }
489 
497 inline unsigned int mapDoubleToUINT(double value, double min, double max, int minMap, int maxMap, bool roundValue = false)
498 {
499  // --- bound to limits
500  value = fmin(value, max);
501  value = fmax(value, min);
502 
503  // --- map to range
504  unsigned int mappedValue = 0;
505  double mapped = (double(value - min) / double(max - min)) * double(maxMap - minMap) + double(minMap);
506  if (roundValue)
507  mappedValue = (unsigned int)(round(mapped));
508  else
509  mappedValue = (unsigned int)mapped;
510 
511  return mappedValue;
512 }
513 
519 inline double mapUINTToDouble(unsigned int value, unsigned int min, unsigned int max, double minMap, double maxMap)
520 {
521  // --- bound to limits
522  value = fmin(value, max);
523  value = fmax(value, min);
524 
525  double mapped = (double(value - min) / double(max - min)) * double(maxMap - minMap) + double(minMap);
526  return mapped;
527 }

534 inline double midi14_bitToBipolar(uint32_t midiDataLSB, uint32_t midiDataMSB)
535 {
536  // --- combine data, LSB or-ed with MSB left-shifted by 7
537  int midi14_bitValue = (int)((midiDataLSB & 0x7F) | ((midiDataMSB & 0x7F) << 7));
538 
539  // --- convert to bipolar (0x2000 = 8192)
540  return (double)(midi14_bitValue - 0x2000) / (double)(0x2000);
541 }

549 inline uint32_t midi14_bitToUnipolarInt(uint32_t midiDataLSB, uint32_t midiDataMSB)
550 {
551  // --- combine data, LSB or-ed with MSB left-shifted by 7
552  uint32_t midi14_bitValue = (uint32_t)((midiDataLSB & 0x7F) | ((midiDataMSB & 0x7F) << 7));
553  return midi14_bitValue;
554 }

561 inline double midi14_bitToUnipolarDouble(uint32_t midiDataLSB, uint32_t midiDataMSB)
562 {
563  // --- combine data, LSB or-ed with MSB left-shifted by 7
564  uint32_t midi14_bitValue = (uint32_t)((midiDataLSB & 0x7F) | ((midiDataMSB & 0x7F) << 7));
565 
566  // --- normalize 0x4000 = 16384
567  return (double)(midi14_bitValue) / (double)(0x4000);
568 }
569 
575 inline double midi14_bitToDouble(uint32_t midiDataLSB, uint32_t midiDataMSB, double minValue, double maxValue)
576 {
577  // --- combine data, LSB or-ed with MSB left-shifted by 7
578  uint32_t midi14_bitValue = (uint32_t)((midiDataLSB & 0x7F) | ((midiDataMSB & 0x7F) << 7));
579 
580  // --- normalize 0x4000 = 16384
581  double value = (double)(midi14_bitValue) / (double)(0x4000);
582 
583  mapDoubleValue(value, 0.0, 1.0, minValue, maxValue);
584  return value;
585 }

594 inline void unipolarIntToMIDI14_bit(uint32_t unipolarValue, uint32_t& midiDataLSB, uint32_t& midiDataMSB)
595 {
596  // --- convert to 16-bit unsigned short
597  unsigned short shValue = (unsigned short)unipolarValue;
598  unsigned short shd1 = shValue & 0x007F;
599 
600  // --- shift back by 1
601  unsigned short shd2 = shValue << 1;
602 
603  // --- split into MSB, LSB
604  shd2 = shd2 & 0x7F00;
605 
606  // --- shift MSB back to fill LSB position
607  shd2 = shd2 >> 8;
608 
609  // --- copy into unsigned ints, fill lower portions
610  midiDataLSB = shd1;
611  midiDataMSB = shd2;
612 }
613 
614 
620 inline void bipolarIntToMIDI14_bit(int32_t biPolarValue, int32_t minValue, int32_t maxValue, uint32_t& midiDataLSB, uint32_t& midiDataMSB)
621 {
622  // --- convert bipolar value to 14-bit value
623  mapIntValue(biPolarValue, minValue, maxValue, 0, 16383);
624 
625  // --- convert to 16-bit unsigned short
626  unsigned short shValue = (unsigned short)biPolarValue;
627  unsigned short shd1 = shValue & 0x007F;
628 
629  // --- shift back by 1
630  unsigned short shd2 = shValue << 1;
631 
632  // --- split into MSB, LSB
633  shd2 = shd2 & 0x7F00;
634 
635  // --- shift MSB back to fill LSB position
636  shd2 = shd2 >> 8;
637 
638  // --- copy into unsigned ints, fill lower portions
639  midiDataLSB = shd1;
640  midiDataMSB = shd2;
641 }

649 inline void unipolarDoubleToMIDI14_bit(double unipolarValue, uint32_t& midiDataLSB, uint32_t& midiDataMSB)
650 {
651  // --- should never happen, but needed
652  boundValue(unipolarValue, 0.0, 1.0);
653 
654  // --- convert to 16-bit unsigned short
655  unsigned short shValue = (unsigned short)(unipolarValue * (double)(0x4000));
656  unsigned short shd1 = shValue & 0x007F;
657 
658  // --- shift back by 1
659  unsigned short shd2 = shValue << 1;
660 
661  // --- split into MSB, LSB
662  shd2 = shd2 & 0x7F00;
663 
664  // --- shift MSB back to fill LSB position
665  shd2 = shd2 >> 8;
666 
667  // --- copy into unsigned ints, fill lower portions
668  midiDataLSB = shd1;
669  midiDataMSB = shd2;
670 }

690 inline double pitchShiftTableLookup(double semitones)
691 {
692  double index = kPitchShiftTableCenter + (semitones*kPitchShiftTableCenterSemis);
693  if (index >= kPitchShiftTableEnd) return pitchShiftTable[kPitchShiftTableEnd];
694  int intPart = (int)index;
695  return doLinearInterpolation(0.0, 1.0, pitchShiftTable[intPart], pitchShiftTable[intPart + 1], index - intPart);
696 }

707 inline uint32_t midiNoteNumberFromOscFrequency(double oscillatorFrequency, double frequencyA440 = 440.0)
708 {
709  // --- ceil will round up
710  double midiNote = ceil(12.0*log2(oscillatorFrequency / frequencyA440) + 69.0); //--- 69 = MIDI note # for A-440
711 
712  // --- grab int part
713  uint32_t renderMidiNoteNumber = (uint32_t)(midiNote);
714 
715  // --- bound to 0 -> 127
716  boundMIDIValueByte(renderMidiNoteNumber);
717 
718  return renderMidiNoteNumber;
719 }
720 
730 inline double midiNoteNumberToOscFrequency(uint32_t midiNoteNumber, double frequencyA440 = 440.0)
731 {
732  // --- https://newt.phys.unsw.edu.au/jw/notes.html
733  double pitch = pow(2.0, (((double)midiNoteNumber - 69.0) / 12.0))*frequencyA440;
734 
735  return pitch;
736 }

739 inline double calculateWaveTablePhaseInc(double oscFrequency, double sampleRate, uint32_t wavetableLength)
740 {
741  // --- for wavetables, inc = (kWaveTableLength)*(fo/fs)
742  return wavetableLength*(oscFrequency / sampleRate);
743 }

746 inline bool checkAndWrapWaveTableIndex(double& index, unsigned int tableLength)
747 {
748  if (index > tableLength)
749  {
750  index = fmod(index, tableLength);
751  return true;
752  }
753  else if (index < 0.0)
754  {
755  index = tableLength + fmod(index - tableLength, tableLength);
756  return true;
757  }
758 
759  return false;
760 }
761 
762 enum class XFadeType { kLinear, kConstantPower };
763 
769 inline double crossfade(XFadeType xfadeType, double inputA, double inputB, double xFrac)
770 {
771  double output = 0.0;
772 
773  if (xfadeType == XFadeType::kConstantPower)
774  output = inputA*(1.0 - xFrac*xFrac) + inputB*(1.0 - (xFrac - 1.0)*(xFrac - 1.0)); // A gain = 1 - x^2, B gain = 1 - ((x-1)^2)
775  else // linear
776  output = inputA*(1.0 - xFrac + inputB*(xFrac));
777 
778  return output;
779 }
780 
781 inline double semitonesBetweenFrequencies(double startFrequency, double endFrequency)
782 {
783  return log2(endFrequency / startFrequency)*12.0;
784 }

794 struct Timer

805  uint32_t getTargetValueInSamples() { return targetValueInSamples; }

818 struct XHoldFader
819 {
820 public:
821  XHoldFader() {}
822  XHoldFader(double _sampleRate, double _xfadeTime_mSec)
823  {
824  sampleRate = _sampleRate;
825  xfadeTime_mSec = _xfadeTime_mSec;
826  }
827 
828  // --- fader functions
829  void reset() { xfadeTime_Counter = 0; holdTime_Counter = 0; }
830 
831  void setSampleRate(double _sampleRate) { sampleRate = _sampleRate; updateXFadeTime(); updateHoldTime(); }
832  void setXFadeTime_mSec(double _xfadeTime_mSec) { xfadeTime_mSec = _xfadeTime_mSec; updateXFadeTime(); updateHoldTime(); }
833  void setPureXfade(bool _pureCrossfade) { pureCrossfade = _pureCrossfade; }
834 
835  void setSourceHoldTime_mSec(double _holdTime_mSec)
836  {
837  holdTime_mSec = _holdTime_mSec;
838  updateHoldTime();
839  }
840 
841  // --- crossfade FROM A to B
842  bool processInputChannels(double inputA, double inputB, double& output)
843  {
844  if (!pureCrossfade && (holdTime_Counter < holdTime_Samples))
845  {
846  output = inputA;
847  holdTime_Counter++;
848  return false;
849  }
850  else // do crossfade
851  {
852  if (pureCrossfade && xfadeTime_Samples == 0)
853  {
854  output = inputA;
855  holdTime_Counter++;
856  return false;
857  }
858 
859  double x = (double)xfadeTime_Counter / (double)xfadeTime_Samples;
860 
861  // --- if we just rolled over:
862  if (x >= 1.0)
863  {
864  // --- output is all B now
865  output = inputB;
866 
867  xfadeTime_Counter = 0;
868  holdTime_Counter = xfadeTime_Counter;
869  return true; // done
870  }
871 
872  // --- calculate gains
873  output = inputA*(1.0 - x*x) + inputB*(1.0 - (x - 1.0)*(x - 1.0)); // A gain = 1 - x^2, B gain = 1 - ((x-1)^2)
874  xfadeTime_Counter++;
875  holdTime_Counter++;
876 
877  return false;
878  }
879  }
880 
881 protected:
882  double sampleRate = 44100;
883  double xfadeTime_mSec = 100.0;
884  uint32_t xfadeTime_Samples = 4410;
885  uint32_t xfadeTime_Counter = 0;
886 
887  double holdTime_mSec = 1000.0;
888  uint32_t holdTime_Samples = 4410;
889  uint32_t holdTime_Counter = 0;
890 
891  bool pureCrossfade = false;
892 
893  void updateHoldTime()
894  {
895  // --- time = hold time - half the xfade time (or the A xfade time for asymmetry later)
896  holdTime_Samples = uint32_t(((holdTime_mSec*sampleRate) / 1000.0));
897  if (holdTime_Samples < 2 * xfadeTime_Samples)
898  holdTime_Samples = 0;
899 
900  holdTime_Samples = uint32_t(((holdTime_mSec*sampleRate) / 1000.0)) - (xfadeTime_Samples / 2);
901  }
902  void updateXFadeTime()
903  {
904  xfadeTime_Samples = uint32_t(((xfadeTime_mSec*sampleRate) / 1000.0));
905  }
906 };
907 
908 
914 struct XFader
915 {
916 public:
917  XFader() {}
918  XFader(double _xfadeTime_Samples)
919  {
920  xfadeTime_Samples = _xfadeTime_Samples;
921  }
922 
923  // --- fader functions
924  void reset() { xfadeTime_Counter = 0; }
925 
926  void setXFadeTime(double _xfadeTime_Samples)
927  {
928  xfadeTime_Samples = _xfadeTime_Samples;
929  }
930 
931  // --- crossfade FROM A to B
932  // returns TRUE if the crossfade is still going (needs more samples)
933  // FALSE if the crossfade is finished (done)
934  bool crossfade(XFadeType xfadeType, double inputA, double inputB, double& output)
935  {
936  double x = (double)xfadeTime_Counter / (double)xfadeTime_Samples;
937 
938  // --- if we just rolled over:
939  if (x >= 1.0)
940  {
941  // --- output is all B now
942  output = inputB;
943  xfadeTime_Counter = 0;
944  return false;
945  }
946 
947  // --- calculate gains
948  if (xfadeType == XFadeType::kConstantPower)
949  output = inputA*(1.0 - x*x) + inputB*(1.0 - (x - 1.0)*(x - 1.0)); // A gain = 1 - x^2, B gain = 1 - ((x-1)^2)
950  else // linear
951  output = inputA*(1.0 - x) + inputB*(x);
952 
953  xfadeTime_Counter++;
954  return true; // still need xfade
955  }
956 
957 protected:
958  uint32_t xfadeTime_Samples = 4410;
959  uint32_t xfadeTime_Counter = 0;
960 };
961 
967 struct GlideModulator
968 {
969 public:
970  GlideModulator() {}
971  ~GlideModulator() {}
972 
973  // --- setup the timer and incrementer
974  bool start(uint32_t _startMIDINote, uint32_t _endMIDINote, double glideTime_mSec, double sampleRate)
975  {
976  // --- we don't really need to store these?
977  startMIDINote = _startMIDINote;
978  endMIDINote = _endMIDINote;
979 
980  if (startMIDINote == endMIDINote || glideTime_mSec <= 0.0)
981  {
982  timerActive = false;
983  return false;
984  }
985 
986  semitones = (double)startMIDINote - (double)endMIDINote;
987  countDownTimer = 1.0;
988  timerInc = (1000.0 / glideTime_mSec) / sampleRate;
989  timerActive = true;
990  return true;
991  }
992 
993  // --- get next value, decrement counter
994  double getNextGlideModSemitones()
995  {
996  double output = 0.0;
997  if (timerActive)
998  {
999  output = countDownTimer*semitones;
1000 
1001  countDownTimer -= timerInc;
1002  if (countDownTimer <= 0.0)
1003  timerActive = false;
1004  }
1005  return output;
1006  }
1007 
1008 protected:
1009  bool timerActive = false;
1010  double timerInc = 0.0;
1011  double countDownTimer = 1.0;
1012  double semitones = 1.0;
1013  uint32_t startMIDINote = 0;
1014  uint32_t endMIDINote = 0;
1015 };

1030 struct SynthOscParameters
1031 {
1032  SynthOscParameters() {}
1033 
1034  SynthOscParameters& operator=(const SynthOscParameters& params)
1035  {
1036  if (this == &params)
1037  return *this;
1038 
1039  oscillatorBankIndex = params.oscillatorBankIndex;
1040  oscillatorWaveformIndex = params.oscillatorWaveformIndex;
1041 
1042  detuneOctaves = params.detuneOctaves;
1043  detuneSemitones = params.detuneSemitones;
1044  detuneCents = params.detuneCents;
1045  unisonDetuneCents = params.unisonDetuneCents;
1046 
1047  pulseWidth_Pct = params.pulseWidth_Pct;
1048  outputAmplitude = params.outputAmplitude;
1049 
1050  oscillatorShape = params.oscillatorShape;
1051  hardSyncRatio = params.hardSyncRatio;
1052  fmRatio = params.fmRatio;
1053  enableHardSync = params.enableHardSync;
1054  enableFreeRunMode = params.enableFreeRunMode;
1055 
1056  return *this;
1057  }
1058 
1059  // --- this is the index in the oscillator data source (for wavetable)
1060  int32_t oscillatorBankIndex = 0; // max is up to the bank container
1061  int32_t oscillatorWaveformIndex = 0; // max is always 32 for this!!
1062 
1063  // --- detuning values
1064  double detuneOctaves = 0.0; // 1 = up one octave, -1 = down one octave
1065  double detuneSemitones = 0.0; // 1 = up one half-step, -1 = down one half-step
1066 
1067  // --- this is most common for "fat" sounds; it can also be forced during "unison" mode
1068  double detuneCents = 0.0; // 1 = up one cent, -1 = down one cent
1069 
1070  // --- this is a root-detuner for unison mode (could combine with detuneCents but would become tangled)
1071  double unisonDetuneCents = 0.0; // 1 = up one cent, -1 = down one cent
1072 
1073  double pulseWidth_Pct = 50.0; // sqr wave only
1074  double outputAmplitude = 1.0; // raw value, NOT dB
1075 
1076  double oscillatorShape = 0.0; // [-1, +1]
1077 
1078  double hardSyncRatio = 1.0; // [1, +???]
1079  double fmRatio = 1.0; // [1, +???]
1080  bool enableHardSync = false; // [1, +???]
1081  bool enableFreeRunMode = false; // [1, +???]
1082 };
